FROM [pf] AS [p]
LEFT JOIN [Projet] AS [p0] ON [p].[Projet_Id] = [p0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [TypeProjet] AS [t] ON [p0].[id_typeprojet] = [t].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [NOMENCLATURE] AS [n] ON [p0].[Id] = [n].[ProjetId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[DateCreation], [b].[Deleted], [b].[Fini], [b].[Laize], [b].[machine], [b].[MetrageLineaire], [b].[NombreBobins], [b].[Passe], [b].[Pf_id], [b].[QuantiteFini], [b].[QuantiteSupport], [b].[quantite], [b0].[Id] AS [Id0], [b0].[BonId], [b0].[FilePath], [b0].[UploadedAt], [s].[Id] AS [Id1], [s].[Bon_id], [s].[DateAffection], [s].[Pourcentage], [s].[QuantiteUtilise], [s].[ReferenceMP], [s].[TypeId], [s].[Id0] AS [Id00], [s].[Label]
    FROM [bf] AS [b]
    LEFT JOIN [BonFiles] AS [b0] ON [b].[Id] = [b0].[BonId]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Bon_id], [m].[DateAffection], [m].[Pourcentage], [m].[QuantiteUtilise], [m].[ReferenceMP], [m].[TypeId], [t0].[Id] AS [Id0], [t0].[Label]
        FROM [Matiere] AS [m]
        INNER JOIN [typeMatiere] AS [t0] ON [m].[TypeId] = [t0].[Id]
    ) AS [s] ON [b].[Id] = [s].[Bon_id]
) AS [s0] ON [p].[Id] = [s0].[Pf_id]
ORDER BY [p].[Id], [p0].[Id], [t].[Id], [n].[Id], [s0].[Id], [s0].[Id0], [s0].[Id1]

    INNER JOIN [typeMatiere] AS [t] ON [m].[TypeId] = [t].[Id]
